<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobDataView', GridHeight: '800', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeeJobDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '800', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divEmployeeJobDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeeJobDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeeJobDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeeJobDataView", "1");
                    GridSetSelectedItemsOn("EmployeeJobDataView", "");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeeJobDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeeJobDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeeJobDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeeJobDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeeJobDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeeJobDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    $("#btnMassUpdateEmployeeJobs__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeeJobDataView");

        if (!$("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowMassUpdateEmployeeJobs")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassUpdateEmployeeJobs" })
                         .SetIsModal(true)
                         .SetWidth(650)
                         .SetHeight("70%")
                         .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                         .SetonActivate(function () { RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsMassUpdate", null); })
                         .SetTitle("Mass Update Employee Jobs");

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    function IsTxnEncumberAllowed() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsTxnEncumberDateAllowed',
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (response) {
                //debugger;
                if (response.Success === true) {
                    $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val('True');
                }
                else {
                    $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val('Flase');
                }
            }
        });
    }
    $('#btnMassIncrementSalaryScheduleGrade__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        MassIncrementSalarySchedule(false);
    });

    $('#btnMassIncrementSalaryScheduleStep__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        MassIncrementSalarySchedule(true);
    });

    function MassIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds == "undefined" || selectedRowIds == null || selectedRowIds.length == 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        var heading = isStepUp ? "Increment Salary Schedule Step" : "Increment Salary Schedule Grade";
        var message = isStepUp ? "Are you sure you want to Increment Salary Schedule Step the selected job(s)?" : "Are you sure you want to Increment Salary Schedule Grade the selected job(s)?";
        PerformIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp, selectedRowIds, heading, message);
    }

    function PerformIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp, selectedRowIds, heading, message) {
        if (isStepUp) {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncrementSalarySchedule")
            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IncrementSalaryScheduleStepPopup?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;isStepUp=" + isStepUp })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle(heading)
        .SetWidth(600)
        .SetHeight("25%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobDataView", null);

        }
        else {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncrementSalarySchedule")
            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IncrementSalaryScheduleGradePopup?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;isStepUp=" + isStepUp })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle(heading)
        .SetWidth(600)
        .SetHeight("25%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobDataView", null);
        }

    }

    function EditEmployeeJob(EmployeeId, CycleId, JobSequence) {

        var id = EmployeeId + '~' + CycleId + '~' + JobSequence;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data;

        data = { Id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, origin: 2 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob", data: data, type: "POST" };

    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowEmployeeJob")
      .SetIsModal(true)
      .SetContent(options)
      .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
      .SetTitle('Edit Employee Job')
      .SetWidth('1220')
      .SetHeight('90%')
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsDataView", null);
    }

    function OnPageLoad() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeeJobDataView");
        $("#btnAdd__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowEmployeeJob")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/CreateJob" + "?employeeID=0&amp;origin=2" })
           .SetTitle('Add Employee Job')
           .SetWidth('1220')
           .SetHeight('90%')
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsDataView", null);
        });

        $("#btnEdit__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var grid = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
            if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
                var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
            }
        });

        $("#btnDelete__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?", function () { DeleteEmployeeJob(); });
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }
        });

        var submitForAllNo = false;
        var submitForAllYes = false;
        $('#btnApproveJob__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            submitForAllNo = false;
            submitForAllYes = false;

            var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
                return;
            }

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
                ShowYesNoDialog("Approve Job", "Are you sure you want to approve the selected job(s)?", function () { ApproveJobDialogue(); });
            }
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }

        });

    }
    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;

    function RefreshOnApproveJobs(jobID, inProcessRegisterWarning, moveNext, overbudget) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var key = '';
        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
                     { jobID: jobID, moveNext: moveNext, massOpertaionId: massOperationId, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, overbudget: overbudget, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                key, function (result) {

                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, false);

                    }

                    else if (result.Success == 3) {
                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false);
                        }
                        else {

                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false); submitForAllNo = e; });
                        }
                    }

                    else if (result.Success == 5) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true);
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true); submitForAllNo = e; });

                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {
                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');

                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);
    }

    function ApproveJobDialogue() {
        // check if the config values are present, if yes then show the dialogue.
        var showTransactionDatesPopup = $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val();

        var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView"), origin: "2" };
        //var encumberWages = false;
        aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJobWages",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                alert(error);
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                    ShowApproveJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ApproveJobEnterDate");
                }
                else {
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnApproveJobs(-1, true, false, false); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ShowApproveJobDatePopup(contentURL) {

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("EmployeeJobsManageApproveJobDatePopup")
            .SetContent({ url: contentURL })
            .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
            .SetTitle('Approve Job(s)')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeApproveJobDate", null);

    }

    function RefreshOnCloseEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        var key = '';
        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseEmployeeJob',
                     { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                key, function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    $("#btnCloseJob__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
            ShowYesNoDialog("Close Job", "Are you sure you want to close the selected job(s)?", function () {
                var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
                var showTransactionDatesPopup = $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val();

                var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
                var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView"), origin: "2" };
                var encumberWages = false;
                aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
                    url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJob",
                    data: data,
                    dataType: "json",
                    error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                        alert(error);
                    },
                    success: function (result) {
                        if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                            ShowCloseJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseJobEnterDate");
                        }
                        else {
                            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnCloseEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds); });
                            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                        }
                    }
                });

            });
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });

    function ShowCloseJobDatePopup(contentURL) {

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("EmployeeJobsManageCloseJobDatePopup")
            .SetContent({ url: contentURL })
            .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
            .SetTitle('Close Job(s)')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeCloseJobDate", null);

    }

    $("#btnFillPosition__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function () {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowFillPosition")
            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/FillPositionDetails?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;dataViewName=EmployeeJobDataView" })
            .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
            .SetTitle('Fill Position')
            .SetWidth(550)
            .SetHeight(190)
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeFillPosition", null);

    });

    $("#btnVacatePosition__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
            ShowYesNoDialog("Vacate Position", "Are you sure that you want to vacate the positions associated with all of the selected jobs?", function () { VacatePosition(); });
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });

    $("#btnViewPositionManagement__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function () {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ViewPositionManagement?" + "jobId=" + selectedRowIds;
    });

    function RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeJob',
                    { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteEmployeeJob() {

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    };

    function ApproveJobsWithWarning(inProcessRegisterWarning) {

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        // debugger;
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, origin: "2" },
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job approved successfully.", "success");

                    //removing selection from the attributes.
                    grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function VacatePosition() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var data = { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") };
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/VacatePositionEmployeeJob',
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job vacated successfully.", "success");

                    //removing selection from the attributes.
                    grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                    grid.thead.find("tr .selectAll__EmployeeJobDataView").attr("checked", false);
                    SetGridSelectedRecords("EmployeeJobDataView", "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    };

    function MassApproveJobs() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/QAAutom/Employee/IsActiveJobInMassApproveSelectedEmployees",
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (returnData) {
                //debugger;
                if (!returnData) {
                    //redirect to Mass Job approve grid
                    window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob?fromSearch=False";
                }
                else {
                    ShowYesNoDialog("Mass Approve", "One or more of the selected jobs may be part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed. Any changes that have been made to the job(s) will not affect this register. To have the changes apply to the in-process register, the job(s) will have to be removed from the register before running this process. Do you want to continue with the Mass Job Approval?", function () {
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob?fromSearch=False";
                    });
                }

            },
            error: function (e) {
                //debugger;
            }
        });

    }

    $('#btnMassApproveJob__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function () {

        MassApproveJobs();
    });

    $('#btnRolloverEmployeeJobs__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd();
    });

    function OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd() {

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsNextCycleAvailable',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "No next cycle available for rollover job process.", null);
                    return;
                }
                var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowRolloverEmployeeJob")
                            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/RolloverEmployeeJob" }).SetIsModal(true).SetHeight(430).SetWidth(640)
                .SetTitle('Rollover Employee Jobs').SetonDeactivate(function () { UnRegisterActiveScreen(); });
                finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            }
        });

    }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
